<script>
HideBrowserBasedLinks();
function HideBrowserBasedLinks(){
	var clss1 = "force-download-IE";
	var clss2 = "force-download-non-IE";
	var version = detectIE();
	
	if(version === false){
		hideClass = clss1;
	}else{hideClass = clss2;}
	
	var links = document.getElementsByClassName(hideClass);
	for(var i = 0; i < links.length; i++){
		links[i].style = "display: none !important;";
		links[i].setAttribute("style","display: none !important;");
	}
}

function detectIE() {
  var ua = window.navigator.userAgent;
  var msie = ua.indexOf('MSIE ');
  if (msie > 0) {
    return parseInt(ua.substring(msie + 5, ua.indexOf('.', msie)), 10);
  }

  var trident = ua.indexOf('Trident/');
  if (trident > 0) {
    var rv = ua.indexOf('rv:');
    return parseInt(ua.substring(rv + 3, ua.indexOf('.', rv)), 10);
  }

  var edge = ua.indexOf('Edge/');
  if (edge > 0) {
    return parseInt(ua.substring(edge + 5, ua.indexOf('.', edge)), 10);
  }
  return false;
}
</script><script>
(() => {
    document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function () {

      $.ajax({
        url: "/advisorsites/investoraccess/decryptusername",
        method: "GET",
        dataType: "json",
        success: function (data) {
          const { DecryptedUsername: username } = data;
          if (!username) {
            return;
          }
          if ($('[name="LoginName"]')[2]) {
            $('[name="LoginName"]')[2].value = username;
          }
          if ($('[name="LoginName"]')[4]) {
            $('[name="LoginName"]')[4].value = username;
          }
        },
        error: function (error) {
          console.error(error);
        },
      });

      const first = $(".ia-checkbox-label")[2];
      const firstCheckbox = first.previousElementSibling;
      const second = $(".ia-checkbox-label")[4];
      const secondCheckbox = second?.previousElementSibling;
      if (first) {
        first.addEventListener("click", function (e) {
          e.preventDefault();
          firstCheckbox.checked = !firstCheckbox.checked;
        });
      }
  
      if (!second) {
        return;
      }
      second.addEventListener("click", function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        secondCheckbox.checked = !secondCheckbox.checked;
      });
    });
  })();
</script><script>
;(function() {
    const iframes = document.querySelectorAll('.mwEmbedKalturaIframe');

    if(!iframes){
        return;
    }

    iframes.forEach((iframe, index) => {
        iframe.title = `Kaltura Player ${++index}`;
    });
})();

;(() => {
    const images = document.querySelectorAll('img')

    if(!images){
        return;
    }
    
    images.forEach(image => {
        if(!image.hasAttribute('alt') || image.getAttribute('alt') === ' ') {
            image.setAttribute('alt', '');
        }
    });
})();
